### Post by cardinals_fan on 2008-07-29
> **What is in a name? said:**
> Could you share your .conkyrc with us, please? Thanks in advance.

That's an old .conkyrc that I resurrected because my current one doesn't go well with that wallpaper.  The code is below:```
#.conkyrc
#cardinals_fan
#4/6/2008

# Create own window instead of using desktop (required in nautilus)
own_window yes
own_window_type override
own_window_type desktop
own_window_transparent 1
own_window_hints undecorated,below,skip_taskbar,skip_pager

# Use double buffering (reduces flicker, may not work for everyone)
double_buffer yes

# fiddle with window
use_spacer none
use_xft yes

# Update interval in seconds
update_interval 3.0

# Minimum size of text area
# minimum_size 250 5

# Draw shades?
draw_shades no

# Text stuff
draw_outline no # amplifies text if yes
draw_borders no
uppercase no # set to yes if you want all text to be in uppercase

# Use Xft?
use_xft yes

# Xft font when Xft is enabled
xftfont HandleGotD:size=10

# Text alpha when using Xft
xftalpha 0.5

# Stippled borders?
stippled_borders 8

# border margins
border_margin 4

# border width
border_width 1

# Default colors and also border colors, grey90 == #e5e5e5
default_color grey

own_window_colour brown
own_window_transparent yes

# Text alignment, other possible values are commented
#alignment top_left
#alignment top_right
#alignment bottom_left
alignment bottom_right

# Gap between borders of screen and text
gap_x 10
gap_y 10

# stuff after 'TEXT' will be formatted on screen

TEXT
${offset -2}${voffset 105}${color c90006}${font HeldustryFTVBasic Demi:size=80}${time %H}
${offset 115}${voffset -153}${font HeldustryFTVBasic Demi:size=34}${time %M}
${offset 121}${voffset -25}${color 9d9d9d}${font HandleGotD:size=16}${time %b}
${offset 120}${voffset -5}${time %d}
${offset 10}${voffset 20}${color 9d9d9d}${font HeldustryFTVBasic Demi:size=16}CPU: $cpu%
${offset 10}${voffset 5}${color 9d9d9d}${font HeldustryFTVBasic Demi:size=16}RAM: $memperc%

```

### Post by etnlIcarus on 2008-07-30
> **myusername said:**
> i have a question....could u run awn in xubuntu without compiz since xfce has a built in compositor? or how about metacity since it has one nowI don't think it matters whether you're using a compositor. Just so long as your system supports compositing. If AWN were dependent upon the compositor, it would be mightly slow under Xfwm's compositor, since it lacks hardware acceleration.

> **RiceMonster said:**
> Giving Xfce a better try and liking it so far. I'm actually using a panel and I actually like it with Xfce. I might actually switch out of Openbox. Also trying out a dark theme to match my joker wallpaper.

Info in the terminal.
Yeah, I was surprised at how much more elegant xfce4-panel is, compared to kicker or gnome-panel. It's not as customisable (you don't appear to be able to set a panel to appear under other windows. God, that's pissing me off) but configuration and use are really smooth.

---

### Post by RiceMonster on 2008-07-30
> **etnlIcarus said:**
> Yeah, I was surprised at how much more elegant xfce4-panel is, compared to kicker or gnome-panel. It's not as customisable (you don't appear to be able to set a panel to appear under other windows. God, that's pissing me off) but configuration and use are really smooth.

Yeah, it's very nice. It seems to annoy me a lot less than the other panels I've used, though I really don't know why. I'm also glad that it's got scrollable desktops and right-click on desktop = root menu. I find it hard to live without those.

### Post by Killeroid on 2008-07-30
So here's mine. 

[[IMG]http://farm4.static.flickr.com/3120/2715481865_52dc9194e9.jpg[/IMG]]("http://farm4.static.flickr.com/3120/2715481865_84652b0804_o.png")

and 

[[IMG]http://farm4.static.flickr.com/3239/2715488903_2b8b7a599b.jpg[/IMG]]("http://farm4.static.flickr.com/3239/2715488903_baee92978f_o.png")

GTK/Metacity : **[Elegant Blue]("http://gnome-look.org/content/show.php/Elegant-Blue?content=85622")**
Wallpaper:     **[Joker Wallpaper]("http://flickr.com/photos/killeroid/2716334564/")**
Icon:          **[Eikon]("http://www.mediafire.com/?mw1diuef9yx")**
Font:          Calibri

Ubuntu 8.04, using tint2 for taskbar and trayer for notification area. I got rid of gnome-panel by going to Sessions-->Current Session and remove gnome panel from the list of running applications, then going to Session Options and clicking on the Remember button.Gnome-panel will not restart next time you log in.

To start trayer as shown in my screenshot:
```
trayer --edge bottom --align right --widthtype request --height 18 --expand false --transparent true --alpha 255 --margin 8 --distance 8
```

My tintrc:
```

#---------------------------------------------
# TINT CONFIG FILE
#---------------------------------------------

#---------------------------------------------
# PANEL
#---------------------------------------------
panel_mode = multi_desktop
panel_monitor = 1
panel_position = bottom center
panel_size = 1100 34
panel_margin = 0 0
panel_padding = 5 5
font_shadow = 0

#---------------------------------------------
# PANEL BACKGROUND AND BORDER
#---------------------------------------------
panel_rounded = 9
panel_border_width = 2
panel_background_color = #000000 0
panel_border_color = #000000 0

#---------------------------------------------
# TASKS
#---------------------------------------------
task_text_centered = 1
task_width = 200
task_margin = 2
task_padding = 2
task_icon_size = 0
task_font = Calibri bold 8
task_font_color = #ffffff 59
task_active_font_color = #ffffff 90

#---------------------------------------------
# TASK BACKGROUND AND BORDER
#---------------------------------------------
task_rounded = 3
task_background_color = #000000 40
task_active_background_color = #000000 55
task_border_width = 1
task_border_color = #d1d1d1 34
task_active_border_color = #d1d1d1 40

#---------------------------------------------
# CLOCK
#---------------------------------------------
time1_format = %H:%M
time1_font = Calibri bold 8
time2_format = %A %d %B
time2_font = Calibri bold 6
clock_font_color = #ffffff 90

#---------------------------------------------
# MOUSE ACTION ON TASK
#---------------------------------------------
mouse_middle = close
mouse_right = none
mouse_scroll_up = toggle
mouse_scroll_down = iconify


```

This whole setup inspired by an xfce desktop screenshot I saw posted in one of the screenshot threads.

> **fedex1993 said:**
> can i get your conky config?
Here's the clock conky:```
double_buffer yes
update_interval 1.0
background yes

own_window yes
own_window_transparent yes
own_window_type root
own_window_hints undecorated,below,sticky,skip_taskbar,skip_pager

use_xft yes
override_utf8_locale no
xftfont Bitstream Vera Sans:size=9
xftalpha 0.8
draw_shades no
draw_outline no
draw_borders no
uppercase no
use_spacer no

border_margin 9
border_width 0

default_color white
default_outline_color black

alignment top_left
gap_x 9
gap_y 6

TEXT
${font Mono:size=50}${offset 530}${voffset 38}${time %H:%M}${font}

```
and the bottom conky:```
double_buffer yes
update_interval 3.0
background yes

own_window yes
own_window_transparent yes
own_window_type root
own_window_hints undecorated,below,sticky,skip_taskbar,skip_pager

minimum_size 0 0
maximum_width 1280

use_xft yes
override_utf8_locale no
xftfont Bitstream Vera Sans:size=9
xftalpha 0.8
draw_shades no
draw_outline no
draw_borders no
uppercase no
use_spacer no

border_margin 0
border_width 0

default_color white
default_outline_color black

alignment bottom_left
gap_x 3
gap_y 3

TEXT
${voffset 81}
${voffset -35}${font :size=10}CPU ${cpu}% ${acpitemp}C
${cpugraph 16,200 009900 009900}
${font :size=10}Ram ${memperc}% ${mem}/${memmax}${offset 35}${font}
${membar 16,200}

```

> BEAUTIFUL! xfce? can u post links?

Xfce indeed. My favourite.

The wallpaper was downloaded from DeviantArt: [http://mazdabation.deviantart.com/art/Reise-Reise-16808779](http://mazdabation.deviantart.com/art/Reise-Reise-16808779)
All I did was to cut off the margins a bit. Personal taste.

The GTK theme is from my most recent pack of themes, called Glow: [http://gnome-look.org/content/show.php/Glow?content=85996](http://gnome-look.org/content/show.php/Glow?content=85996)

The Xfwm4 was a kind contribution from another person on Xfce-look: [http://www.xfce-look.org/content/show.php/Glow+xfwm4?content=86083](http://www.xfce-look.org/content/show.php/Glow+xfwm4?content=86083)

If there's anything else you need, just ask. :)

### Post by What is in a name? on 2008-07-30
> **myusername said:**
> okay so i tried installing the aurora engine from here
[http://xfce-look.org/content/show.php/Aurora+Gtk+Engine?content=56438](http://xfce-look.org/content/show.php/Aurora+Gtk+Engine?content=56438)

and i got this output
checking for GTK... no
configure: error: GTK+-2.10 is required to compile aurora
andrew@Xubuntu:~/56438-Aurora-1.4/aurora-1.4$

To compile stuff you need the dev equivalents of some packages. 
How about installing libgtk2.0-dev and then trying to compile Aurora again?

### Post by Arathorn on 2008-07-31
[]("http://img.photobucket.com/albums/v334/mfmeulenbelt/schemrafdruk.png")It's KDE 4.1 with the Arezzo plasma theme and the Oxygen window decoration (without the ugly stripes) and icons.
The wallpaper is from [Florian Freundt]("http://florian.freundt.org/W_Vector.html") (I have three of them to rotate every five minutes) and I use [Legendum]("http://home.kabelfoon.nl/%7Eslam/fonts/fonts.html") as system font. All in all pretty straightforward but the idea is to look beautiful without distracting me from my work.

---

### Post by Arathorn on 2008-07-31
> **UrbanSlayer said:**
> Very nice.  How did you remove the stripes from the Oxygen window decoration?
It's an option in the system settings. If you select Oxygen as window decoration, there's a check box for the stripes right under it.
